#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()

    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ra;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;

#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ra;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).rg;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ar;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).gr;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform samplerExternalOES u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;

#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
uniform vec3 u_offset;
uniform mat3 u_matrix;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ra;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += u_offset;
    rgb = yuv * u_matrix;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
